 coffee kaa facialchehare par chamak laane ke liye vaise to market main ek se badhkar ek beauty product milte hai

 Coffee works by removing dead skin from the face, which softens the skin and enhances facial glow
 coffee facial kii saamagreeek katori main 1 chammach coffee powder len
 Now add a little rice flour to it
 chaaval kaa aataa aap market se kharid sakati hai
 If you want, you can also make rice by grinding it
 ab isamen 2 chammach kaccha doodh, ek chammach neembu kaa ras or ek chammach shahad milaayein

 # Highlights 1: pashchim bengal, tamilnadu, assam, kerala or puducheri main vidhansabha chunaav ke liye aaj voton kii ginati hogi
 # dilli sarkaar ke bajet main mahila ayog ko khaas tavajjo di gai
 The budget of Delhi Women's Commission has been increased three times
 bajet saat karod se badhkar 20 karod ho gaya
 Swati Maliwal, chairman of the Delhi Women's Commission, said that the cyber cell will be opened in Delhi soon
 jahaan mahilaon se judi shikaayatein darj kar karrwai kii jaaegi
 Swati Maliwal said that after increasing the budget, one-stop centers will also be opened in Delhi
 jahaan mahila ayog, dilli police or vakeelon kii team hogi jomahila surakshase jude maamle darj us par karrwai karegi
 According to Swati Maliwal, the Delhi Commission for Women will now plan to open a women's panchayat across the state
 mahila panchayaton ke jariye mohalla str par mahilaon kii suraksha sunishchit karai jaaegi
 Swati said that there was a demand for an increase in the budget to carry out the increasing work of the Women's Commission
 jharkhand ke rajyapal said sibte raji in dinon chunaav ayog kii nigahon main hai
 Reason, to take important decisions after the Model Code of Conduct comes into force
 par ve us samay bachaav kii mudra main aa gaye jab chunaav ayog ne kaha ki rajyapal kii kaaryakari bhoomika adarsh aachaar samhita ke daayre main aati he
 It is like this, on March 23, the Governor's Advisory Committee announced a 6 percent increase in dearness allowance for state government employees
 is masale ko bhaajapa chunaav ayog ke samaksh le gai
 Election Commissioner S
 vaai
 When Qureshi came to Ranchi last week, he said that the executive role of the governor comes under the model code of conduct
 rajya sarkaar ke karmchaariyon ke mahangaai bhatte main vruddhi karne se pehle anumati lee jaani chahie thi
 Debashish Gupta, Chief Election Commissioner, Jharkhand, said, "the Governor's Advisory Committee had not taken any permission before the hike in DA
 '' chunaav ayog ne jab is mudde par naaraazgi jataai to vitt vibhaag ne mahangaai bhatte main vruddhi par 29 march ko roak laga di
 Now the case of dearness allowance was about to calm down that the role of the Governor came into the radar of the Election Commission even once
 30 march ko rajyapal kii salaahkaar samiti ne baithak kii
 91 crore to infuse Heavy Engineering Corporation (HEC) in this meeting
 kaa check jari karne kaa faisla liya gaya
 The check was handed over to HEC management on Tuesday
 ye 91 karod ru
 250 crores sanctioned for the State Government HEC
 ke punaruddhar package ke tahat jari kiye gaye
 The BJP once again objected to the decision of the Governor's Advisory Committee and demanded appropriate action against the Governor
 isamen mjedaar baat yah rahi ki is baar bhi salaahkaar samiti ne chunaav ayog kii anumati lenaa munasib nahin samajha
 When Debashish Gupta was asked about this, he said, "nobody took any permission to issue a check for the revival package of HEC
" echisi ne is baat kii anumati maangi thi ki kya vah rajya sarkaar se package ke tahat mili raashi ko sevanivrutt karmchaariyon main vitarit kar sakati he
 "on this issue, a Rajya Bhavan official said," The Governor's Advisory Committee on February 13 raised Rs 250 crore for the revival of HEC
 ke package kii ghoshnaa kii thi
 That is, this announcement was made a fortnight before the date of elections
 salaahkaar samiti ne usee package kaa ek hissaa bhar jari kiya he
 However, the BJP is not ready to hear any argument on this issue
 uski rajya ikai ke adhyaksh raghubar das kehete hai, ''hamane rajyapal ke khilaaf karrwai karne ke liye chunaav ayog ko likhaa he
 This is the second time the Advisory Committee has violated the Model Code of Conduct
 yah package ranchi se congress ummidavaar subodh kaant sahay ko laabh pahunchane ke uddeshy se he
 He said that to conduct a fair election in the state, the Governor should be removed as soon as possible
 sahay kendriya khaadya prasanskaran mantri hai
 They are claiming in their rallies that they have ensured a revival package for the people of HEC and are engaged in reviving the ailing company
 echisi ghate kii company thi lekin pichley teen saal se ye lagaataar phaayde main ja rahi he
 Congress leaders are claiming that it is their government at the Center that has carried out this revival
 echisi main lagbhag 6,000 karmchaaree hai joki chunaav main kisi bhi ummidavaar kii sambhaavnaaon main kaaphi bada badlaav laa sakate hai
 The STF of Uttar Pradesh has exposed the racket of oil theft by raiding several petrol pumps in Lucknow
 is karrwai se sabit hua he ki kaise graahak petrol panpon par thage jate hai
 Tells you ways that you can avoid this fraud
 1-check karte rahen milagepetrol churaane ke liye pump maalik aksar pehle se hi meter main herapheri karte hai
 According to the knowledgeable Naresh Taneja, many petrol pumps in the country are still running on old technology in which it is very easy to rig
 niyamon ke mutabik petrol daalane kii mashin main kharabi aane par sirf tel company ke maikenic hi use thik kar sakate hai
 But owners of petrol pumps often seek the help of private mechanics
 mashin main chhedchhad usee vakt hoti he
 So, you can pour oil from different petrol pumps and keep checking the mileage of your car continuously
 2- meter par rakhen najarapane aksar dekha hoga ki petrol panpon par aapako gaadi ko polish karwaane kii peshkash di jaati he
 Or, to divert your attention, an employee would ask whether you would pay the money by card or cash
 mahaj chand secondon ke liye dhyaan hatane par bhi aapako chuunaa lag saktaa he
 So keep an eye on the meter while filling the oil petrol
 3- meter ko riset karwaanaa naa bhuulenkai petrol panpon main karmchaaree aapaki bataai rakam se kam paise kaa tel bharte hai
 Upon interrupting, customers are told that the meter is being reset to zero
 lekin agar aap chaukanne nahin hai to aksar ye meter jiro par nahin laayaa jaataa he
 Therefore, it is important that while filling the oil, make sure that the meter of the petrol pump machine is set to zero
 4- sunishchit karen pipe main bachaa naa rahe petrolapane dekha hoga kai petrol panpon par tel bharne kii pipe ko lanbaa rakhaa jaataa he
 Employees immediately remove the nozzle from the car as soon as it is auto cut after putting petrol
 is vajah se pipe main bachaa hua petrol har baar tank main chalaa jaataa he
 So you should emphasize that the petrol nozzle stays in your vehicle tank for a few seconds after the auto is cut so that the petrol left in the pipe also comes in it
 5- check karen kahin pipe main bal to nahintel dalavaate samay gaadi ko mashin se thodaa dur khadaa karen taaki pipe tana hua rahe or usamen pade bal main tel bachaa naa rah jaae
 6- Do not fill oil by paying the amount of round figure, most people pay petrol or diesel by paying 500, 1000 or 2000
 lekin kai petrol pump maalik ese number ke liye pehle hi mashin ko fiks karke rakhte hai
 Therefore, it is better that you do not fill petrol by paying the round figure
 masalan 530 rupee yaa 1575 rupee kaa petrol bharwane se petrol kii chori kathin hogi or aapaki jeb nahin kategi
 As far as possible, pay with the card
 7-kahin dabaa to nahin rah gaya nojal kaa batan?petrol pump vaale se kahen ki wo tel nikalnaa shuru hone ke baad nojal se haath hataa len
 Pressing the nozzle button while inserting the oil reduces the speed of its discharge and makes it easier to steal
 8- kahin tel kii jagah hawa to nahin bharva rahe aap?tank phul karaate samay auto cat hone ke baad aksar petrol pump vaale round figure main petrol bhar dene kii baat karte hai
 Do not agree to this because after the auto cut, less oil goes into the tank of your vehicle and sometimes due to the machine not being reset, no oil goes at all, that is, only the air goes into your vehicle tank

 Union Environment Minister Jairam Ramesh said in a statement, "in view of the talks with the state government on April 29, the final approval has been given to convert 1,253 hectares of land for Posco project
 " bayaan ke anusaar jile main van kshetra main bekaar padi bhoomi ko unnat yaa upjau banane kaa kharch posco dwaara vahan kiye jane kii shart par manjuuri di gai he
 It is worth mentioning that in January, the environment ministry had given approval to set up the project at Paradip in coastal district Jagatsinghpur
 bhartiya team ko lagaataar do maichon main mili niraashaa ko peeche chhodte hue yahaan sultan ajalan shah cap haaki toornament main bane rahane kii ummiido ko jinda rakhane ke liye chir-pratidwandvi pakistan ke khilaaf agle round robin match main shandaar pradarshan karnaa hoga
 The Indian team, however, can be relieved that the last two matches were very close
 yuva bhartiya team ne shuruaati match main chah baar kii champion australia ke khilaaf 3-4 se haarane se pehle jujharu pradarshan kiya jabaki duusare match main ant main rakshaatmak khaamiyon ke kaaran unhone dakshin korea se 1-2 se match ganvaa diya
 The comments pakistan ne duusari taraf apane abhiyaan kii shuruyaat newjiland ke khilaaf 4-2 kii jeet se kii or beeti raat unhen australia se 0-6 se shikast mili
 After a great performance against Australia, the Indian team was expected to perform well but in the first half of the match against the Korean team, the team completely fell behind, leading Korea to a 1-0 lead
 bhartiya team haalanki is baat se raahat mahasoos kar sakati he ki pichley do match kaaphi kareebi rahe the
 The young Indian team struggled in the opening match before losing 3-4 against six-time champions Australia, while in the second match they lost the match to South Korea 1-2 due to defensive flaws at the end
 tippaniyan Pakistan, on the other hand, started their campaign with a 4–2 win against New Zealand and lost 0–6 to Australia last night
 australia ke khilaaf shandaar pradarshan ke baad bhartiya team se achche pradarshan kii ummid thi lekin korian team ke khilaaf match ke pehle half main team puri tarah pichad gai jisase korea ne 1-0 kii badhat bana lee
 The young Indian team struggled in the opening match before losing 3-4 against six-time champions Australia, while in the second match they lost the match to South Korea 1-2 due to defensive flaws at the end
 tippaniyan Pakistan, on the other hand, started their campaign with a 4–2 win against New Zealand and lost 0–6 to Australia last night
 australia ke khilaaf shandaar pradarshan ke baad bhartiya team se achche pradarshan kii ummid thi lekin korian team ke khilaaf match ke pehle half main team puri tarah pichad gai jisase korea ne 1-0 kii badhat bana lee
 Pakistan, on the other hand, started their campaign with a 4–2 win against New Zealand and lost 0–6 to Australia last night

 pradhanmantri narendra modi kii adhyakshata main hui cabinet kii niyukti kii samiti ne 16 niyuktiyon ko manjuuri di
 Raghav Chandra, a 1982 batch IAS officer of Madhya Pradesh cadre, has been made the head of NHAI
 carmik vibhaag kii ore se jari aadesh ke anusaar air india ke maujuuda pramukh evam prabandh nideshak rohit nandan kaushal vibhaag main sachiv ke taur par aroda kaa sthaan lenge
 Deputy Election Commissioner Vinod Jutsi has been made the new Tourism Secretary
 raay, anjuli chib duggal kaa sthaan lenge jinhen is saal kii shuruyaat main karporate kaary mantralay kaa sachiv banaaya gaya tha
 Now Duggal has been made Secretary in the Department of Financial Services in the Ministry of Finance, who will replace Hasmukh Adhia
 adhiya rajasav sachiv ban rahe hai

 das 1980 batch ke tamilnadu cader ke adhikari hai

 varisht iees adhikari sunil aroda ko aaj soochna evam prasaaran mantralay main nayaa sachiv niyukt kiya gaya
 He is going to replace Vimal Julka
 aroda rajasthan cader ke 1980 batch ke iees adhikari hai

 The Cabinet Appointments Committee chaired by Prime Minister Narendra Modi approved 16 appointments
 madhya pradesh cader ke 1982 batch ke iees adhikari raghav chandra ko enechaeai kaa pramukh banaaya gaya he
 According to an order issued by the Personnel Department, the current Chief and Managing Director of Air India, Rohit Nandan will replace Arora as Secretary in the skills department
 up chunaav ayukta vinod jutsi ko nayaa paryaton sachiv banaaya gaya he
 Rai will succeed Anjuli Chib Duggal, who was made secretary of the Ministry of Corporate Affairs earlier this year
 ab duggal ko vitt mantralay main vittiya seva vibhaag main sachiv banaaya gaya he jo hasmukh adhiya kaa sthaan lenge

 Senior IAS officer Sunil Arora was today appointed as the new Secretary in the Ministry of Information and Broadcasting
 vah vimal julka kaa sthaan lene ja rahe hai
 Arora is a 1980 batch IAS officer of Rajasthan cadre
 philhal vah kaushal vikaas evam udhyamita mantralay ke sachiv hai
 He was appointed at a time when the Ministry of Information and Broadcasting was involved in a number of activities including the e-auction of FM stations of Phase-3 and digitization of Phase-3 and 4
 apatiai-pune ke adhyaksh pad par gajendra chouhan kii niyukti ko lekar bhi mantralay aalochana se ghira hua he
 Arora has also served as CMD in Air India
 tippaniyan JS Deepak Kumar and Shankar Madan will be the new secretaries in the Department of Electronic and Information Technology and the Department of Land Resources
 ajit em sharan ko aayush sachiv banaaya gaya he
 Rajiv Yadav, a 1981 batch IAS officer, will be the new Sports Secretary
